[30;1m52 | [0m[35m        **passthru-undefined-exprs**[0m
[30;1m53 | [0m[35m          This is one of the most powerful pass through algorithms. If an expression passed to[0m
[30;1m54 | [0m[35m          :c:`#if` (or its brethern) contains an unknown macro, expand the expression with[0m
[30;1m55 | [0m[35m          known macros and pass through *unexecuted*, and then pass through the remaining block.[0m
[30;1m56 | [0m[35m          Each :c:`#elif` is evaluated in turn and if it does not contain unknown macros, it will be[0m
[30;1m57 | [0m[35m          executed immediately. Finally, any :c:`#else` clause is always passed through *unexecuted*[0m

[30;1m53 | [0m[35m          This is one of the most powerful pass through algorithms. If an expression passed to[0m
[30;1m54 | [0m[35m          :c:`#if` (or its brethern) contains an unknown macro, expand the expression with[0m
[30;1m55 | [0m[35m          known macros and pass through *unexecuted*, and then pass through the remaining block.[0m
[30;1m56 | [0m[35m          Each :c:`#elif` is evaluated in turn and if it does not contain unknown macros, it will be[0m
[30;1m57 | [0m[35m          executed immediately. Finally, any :c:`#else` clause is always passed through *unexecuted*[0m

[30;1m43 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m44 | [0m[35m**passthru-undefined-exprs**[0m
[30;1m45 | [0m[35m  This is one of the most powerful pass through algorithms. If an expression passed to[0m
[30;1m46 | [0m[35m  :c:`#if` (or its brethern) contains an unknown macro, expand the expression with[0m
[30;1m47 | [0m[35m  known macros and pass through *unexecuted*, and then pass through the remaining block.[0m
[30;1m48 | [0m[35m  Each :c:`#elif` is evaluated in turn and if it does not contain unknown macros, it will be[0m
[30;1m49 | [0m[35m  executed immediately. Finally, any :c:`#else` clause is always passed through *unexecuted*.[0m

[30;1m92 | [0m[35mNote that most of this preprocessor was written originally by David Beazley to show[0m
[30;1m93 | [0m[35moff his excellent Python Lex-Yacc library PLY (http://www.dabeaz.com/ply/) and is[0m

[30;1m95 | [0m[35mquestions which have asked for a pure Python C preprocessor implementation. This[0m
[30;1m96 | [0m[35mimplementation fixes a lot of conformance bugs (the original was never intended to[0m
[30;1m97 | [0m[35mrigidly adhere to the C standard) and adds in a test suite based on the C11 preprocessor[0m

[30;1m62 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m63 | [0m[35m**passthru-includes**[0m
[30;1m64 | [0m[35m  Don't expand those ``#include`` whose arguments match the supplied regular expression[0m
[30;1m65 | [0m[35m  into the output, however still execute those includes. This lets you generate output[0m
[30;1m66 | [0m[35m  with macros from nested includes expanded, however those ``#include`` matching[0m
[30;1m67 | [0m[35m  the regular expression are passed through into the output.[0m

[30;1m43 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m44 | [0m[35m**passthru-undefined-exprs**[0m
[30;1m45 | [0m[35m  This is one of the most powerful pass through algorithms. If an expression passed to[0m
[30;1m46 | [0m[35m  :c:`#if` (or its brethern) contains an unknown macro, expand the expression with[0m
[30;1m47 | [0m[35m  known macros and pass through *unexecuted*, and then pass through the remaining block.[0m
[30;1m48 | [0m[35m  Each :c:`#elif` is evaluated in turn and if it does not contain unknown macros, it will be[0m
[30;1m49 | [0m[35m  executed immediately. Finally, any :c:`#else` clause is always passed through *unexecuted*.[0m

[30;1m52 | [0m[35m        **passthru-undefined-exprs**[0m
[30;1m53 | [0m[35m          This is one of the most powerful pass through algorithms. If an expression passed to[0m
[30;1m54 | [0m[35m          :c:`#if` (or its brethern) contains an unknown macro, expand the expression with[0m
[30;1m55 | [0m[35m          known macros and pass through *unexecuted*, and then pass through the remaining block.[0m
